### Physics

- `P1.1`
  Equation:

  \[X_{\mathrm{P1_1}}^{+,\mathrm{phys}} = P_{\mathrm{P1_1}} X_{\mathrm{P1_1}}^{-,\mathrm{phys}}, \qquad P_{\mathrm{P1_1}} = T_{\mathrm{phys}}^{-1} \Phi_{\mathrm{P1_1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}} T_{\mathrm{phys}}\]

  Variable legend: `u` is the wave profile; `U_line` is the contraction-compatible update.
  Reading: cycle completion / triple essence / essence load line.
  Confidence: mixed

  Variable legend: `m in R^12` is the pitch-tension vector; `tau` is post-line tension.
  Reading: cycle completion / triple essence / essence load line.
  Confidence: mixed

### Game Theory

- `P1.1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P1_1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P1_1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P1_1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P1_1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: cycle completion / triple essence / essence load line.
  Confidence: mixed

- `P1.10`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P1_10}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P1_10}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P1_10}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P1_10}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: extraction circuit / circulation circuit / essence load line.
  Confidence: mixed
